<script>
	function goToTopic(topic) {
		var topicMap = applySpecialCharacterMapping(topic); 
		var url = "/xpl/topicbrowse.jsp?topic=" + escape(topicMap);
		window.top.location.href = url;
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

function searchWithin() {
 	var good_query = filterQuery("swr_query");
 	if (good_query) {
 		var swr_query = getFilteredTerms(document.getElementById("swr_query").value);
 		var url_string =  '/xpl/tocresult.jsp?' + '&' + 
    	document.getElementById("oqs").value +'&'
    	+ 'searchWithin'+ '=' + encodeURI(swr_query);
    	url_string +=  '&'  + 'pageNumber' + '='+ '1'+ '&resultAction=REFINE';
    	window.location = url_string;
    } else {
        return;
    }
  }

</script>

<script>
function sortAction(sortTypeValue) {
	var params = {
		punumber: jQuery.url().param('punumber'),
		sortType: sortTypeValue.value,
		topArticlesDate: jQuery.url().param('topArticlesDate')
	};
if (!sortTypeValue.value.length) {
	delete params.sortType;	
}
if (!params.topArticlesDate) {
	delete params.topArticlesDate;	
}
location.href = location.pathname + '?' + jQuery.param(params);
}
	
</script>

						We fabricated an array of organic LED (OLED) pixels on a dome of clear polymer foil. The array is first formed on the flat polymer substrate and then is shaped to the dome. 					<div style="width: auto; overflow: visible;" class="hide abstract RevealContent">
						<p>
						
						Flexible and large area (5 mm &times;80 mm with an active length of 70 mm) position-sensitive detectors (PSDs) deposited onto polymeric substrates (polyimide-Kapton VN) have been fabricated. The optimized structure presented is based on a heterojunction of amorphous silicon (a-Si:H)/ZnO:Al. The sensors were characterized by spectral response, photocurrent dependence as a function of light intensit...

						<p>
						
						We fabricated poly-Si thin-film transistors at 150&deg;C using inductively coupled plasma (ICP) chemical vapor deposition (CVD) and excimer laser annealing (ELA). An Si film deposited by ICP-CVD was recrystallized using ELA, and a poly-Si film with large grains exceeding 5000 &Aring; in diameter was fabricated. 						<p>
						
						DC plasma display panels are fabricated on flexible polyethylene terephtalate (PET) substrates. Each pixel consists of laterally placed anode and cathode electrodes. All electrical elements are formed on a single PET substrate, whereas a second substrate is needed to encapsulate the panel. Silver is used as the metal for each electrode and standard photolithography is used to form each cell. A 150...

<script type="text/javascript">
	function getParameter(paramName) {
	  var searchString = window.location.search.substring(1),
	      i, val, params = searchString.split("&");

	  for (i=0;i<params.length;i++) {
	    val = params[i].split("=");
	    if (val[0] == paramName) {
	      return unescape(val[1]);
	    }
	  }
	  return null;
	}
	
	 function gotoPage(pagenum) {
		 
		 var rowsPerPage=getParameter("rowsPerPage");
		   var url_string = '/xpl/tocresult.jsp?isnumber=31448' + '&' +document.getElementById("oqs").value
		   + '&' + 'pageNumber' + '='+pagenum;
		  var sortType = getParameter("sortType");
	      if(rowsPerPage!=null){
	               url_string+='&'+'rowsPerPage='+rowsPerPage;
	      }
		   if(sortType!=null){
			   url_string+='&'+'sortType' + '='+sortType;
		   }
		   location.href = url_string;
	 }
</script>

<script>

function getCookie(name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	}
	return null;
}

j$('document').ready(function(){
	if(getCookie('legacyUserName')!=null)
	{
		if(IBP_WS_ENABLED_FLAG){
		Modal.refreshLegacyAccountTransition('/xpl/mwLegacyAccountTransition.jsp');
		}
	}
});

</script>
